--cancel & variable
set define off

CREATE TABLE Consumption_Method(
    consumption_method_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    consumption_method_name VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    PRIMARY KEY(consumption_method_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Ingredient(
    ingredient_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    ingredient_name VARCHAR(25) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    ingredient_price NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    ingredient_stock_quantity NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(ingredient_id),   
    CONSTRAINT CHK_ingredient_price CHECK (ingredient_price >= 0),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_ingredient_stock_quantity CHECK (ingredient_stock_quantity >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Menu_Category(
    menu_category_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    menu_category_name VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    PRIMARY KEY(menu_category_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Loyalty_Level(
    loyalty_level_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    loyalty_level_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    cost_membership NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    loyalty_level_discount_rate NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(loyalty_level_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_cost_membership CHECK (cost_membership >= 500)
);

CREATE TABLE Restaurant_Station(
    restaurant_station_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    restaurant_station_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    max_number_of_staff NUMBER(2) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(restaurant_station_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_number_of_staff CHECK (max_number_of_staff >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Food_Delivery_Company (
    company_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    company_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    company_available NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(company_id)
 );

CREATE TABLE Payment_Method(
    payment_method_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    payment_method_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    payment_method_available NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(payment_method_id) 
);

CREATE TABLE Tax(
    tax_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL, 
    tax_name VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    tax_rate NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(tax_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_tax_rate CHECK (tax_rate >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Discount_Code(
    discount_code_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    discount_code_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    discount_rate NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    discount_code_quantity NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    discount_code_start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    discount_code_end_date DATE NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(discount_code_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_discount_rate CHECK (discount_rate >= 0),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_discount_code_quantity CHECK (discount_code_quantity >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Menu_Item(
    menu_item_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    menu_item_name VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
    menu_item_unit_price NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    menu_item_available NUMBER(1) NOT NULL,
    menu_category_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(menu_item_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(menu_category_id) REFERENCES Menu_Category(menu_category_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_menu_item_unit_price CHECK (menu_item_unit_price >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Member(
    member_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    member_email VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    member_phone_number VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    loyalty_level_id NUMBER(4),
    member_date_of_birth DATE NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(member_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(loyalty_level_id) REFERENCES Loyalty_Level(loyalty_level_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_member_email CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(member_email,'^[a-zA-Z]\w+@(\S+)$'))
);

CREATE TABLE Customer(
    customer_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    customer_name VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
    member_id NUMBER(4),
    PRIMARY KEY(customer_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(member_id) REFERENCES Member(member_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Staff(
    staff_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    staff_last_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    staff_first_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    staff_job_title VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    staff_email VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    staff_phone_number VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    staff_date_of_birth DATE NOT NULL,
    staff_date_joined DATE NOT NULL,
    staff_date_resigned DATE NOT NULL,
    staff_monthly_salary NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    restaurant_station_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(staff_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(restaurant_station_id) REFERENCES Restaurant_Station(restaurant_station_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_staff_monthly_salary CHECK (staff_monthly_salary >= 0),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_staff_email CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(staff_email,'^[a-zA-Z]\w+@(\S+)$'))
);

CREATE TABLE Menu_Promotion_Campaign(
    menu_promotion_campaign_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    discount_rate NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    campaign_start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    campaign_end_date DATE NOT NULL,
    campaign_description VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    menu_category_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    consumption_method_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(menu_promotion_campaign_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(menu_category_id) REFERENCES Menu_Category(menu_category_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(consumption_method_id) REFERENCES Consumption_Method(consumption_method_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_promotion_discount_rate CHECK (discount_rate >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Payment(
    payment_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL, 
    payment_method_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    discount_code_id NUMBER(4),
    tax_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    payment_amount NUMBER(10,2) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(payment_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(payment_method_id) REFERENCES Payment_Method(payment_method_id) ,
    FOREIGN KEY(discount_code_id) REFERENCES Discount_Code(discount_code_id) ,
    FOREIGN KEY(tax_id) REFERENCES Tax(tax_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Order_Form(
    order_form_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    table_number NUMBER(4),
    order_date DATE NOT NULL,
    order_time VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, 
    number_customers NUMBER(4),
    order_form_status VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,    
    consumption_method_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    staff_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    customer_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    payment_id NUMBER(4),
    PRIMARY KEY(order_form_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(consumption_method_id) REFERENCES Consumption_Method(consumption_method_id) ,
    FOREIGN KEY(staff_id) REFERENCES Staff(staff_id) ,
    FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES Customer(customer_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(payment_id) REFERENCES Payment(payment_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Order_Item(
    order_item_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL, 
    order_item_quantity NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    menu_item_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    order_form_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(order_item_id, menu_item_id, order_form_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(menu_item_id) REFERENCES Menu_Item(menu_item_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(order_form_id) REFERENCES Order_Form(order_form_id),
    CONSTRAINT CHK_order_item_quantity CHECK (order_item_quantity >= 0)
);

CREATE TABLE Promo_Payment(
    promo_payment_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    menu_promotion_campaign_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    payment_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(promo_payment_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(menu_promotion_campaign_id) REFERENCES Menu_Promotion_Campaign(menu_promotion_campaign_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(payment_id) REFERENCES Payment(payment_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Menu_Item_Ingredient_Record(
    menu_item_ingredient_record_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    menu_item_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    ingredient_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(menu_item_ingredient_record_id, menu_item_id, ingredient_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(menu_item_id) REFERENCES Menu_Item(menu_item_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(ingredient_id) REFERENCES Ingredient(ingredient_id)
);

CREATE TABLE Food_Delivery_Request (
    food_delivery_request_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    order_form_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    company_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(food_delivery_request_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(order_form_id) REFERENCES Order_Form(order_form_id) ,
    FOREIGN KEY(company_id) REFERENCES Food_Delivery_Company(company_id) 
);

CREATE TABLE Preparation_Station_Request(
    preparation_station_request_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    order_item_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    restaurant_station_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    menu_item_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    order_form_id NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY(preparation_station_request_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(order_item_id, menu_item_id, order_form_id) REFERENCES Order_Item(order_item_id, menu_item_id, order_form_id),
    FOREIGN KEY(restaurant_station_id) REFERENCES Restaurant_Station(restaurant_station_id)
);
